---
title: "11.04 wireless connection/boot up issue"
date: 2011-05-24
forum: General Help
---

### Post by Inst on 2011-05-24
Hey guys,

Ever since installing Natty (roughly 2 weeks ago) I've been experiencing some unsuccessful boot-ups. What I mean by that is that my system would take a long time (about 2 minutes or even more) to boot up and when it did eventually boot up, there were no wireless connections in range (even though I'm sure there are 3 or 4, one of which is mine). A reboot of the system would automatically fix it ( I have no idea how, but it works). This doesn't happen all the time, used to happen only occasionally which I could ignore. However, for the last few days it's been happening every day, I have to boot my system twice or even three times to get it to boot properly. I'm relatively new so I don't know what could be causing it, it probably isn't my adapter or the wireless connection itself so it must have something to do with the way it boots up.
Don't know if this is relevant but I'm using ubuntu classic, the problem persists in unity too so I don't think that could be causing any problems.

---

Hi, you should go to log viewer and see what the logs tell you when you are booting up.
